<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>A review of an early performance, with the indication that the vocal score was expected soon from <a href="/wiki/Janet_et_Cotelle" title="Janet et Cotelle">Janet et Cotelle</a> appears in the <i>Journal général d'annonces d'objets d'arts et de la librairie</i>, (3rd Year, Nº3), 10 Janvier 1827.
</p>
